polloi mallon e sophian onomaseian tote otan tina tis sunnoe radios men otiper an manthane manthanonta mala de polla kai asphalos mnemoneuonta otan te to prosphoron ekasto diamnemoneue tis oti gignomenon an prepoi touto de takhu dra tauta gar apanta oi men phusin oi de sophian oi de agkhinoian thesousin phuseos sophon de ontos oudeni touton oudeis ton emphronon ethelesei pote kalein alla men dei phanenai ge tina epistemen en ekhon sophos gignoit an o sophos ontos on kai me monon doxazomenos idomen de khalepo men gar logo pantapasin epikheiroumen eteran parex ton eiremenon eurein e sophia men legoit an ontos te kai eikotos o de labon oute banausos out elithios estai sophos de kai agathos di auten polites te kai arkhon kai arkhomenos endikos estai poleos ama kai emmeles katidomen de tauten proten tis pot ek tes anthropines phuseos episteme mia diexelthousa e me paragenomene ton nun parouson anoetotaton an kai aphronestaton paraskhoito zoon to ton anthropon ou de touto ge panu khalepon to katidein mia gar os eipein pros mian e ton arithmon dousa panti to thneto genei tout an draseien theon d auton mallon e tina tukhen egoumai donta emin sozein emas on de theon egoumai phrazein khre kaiper atopon onta kai pos ouk atopon au pos gar to agathon aition emin sumpanton ou kai tou polu megistou tes phroneseos aition egeisthai dei gegonenai tina de kai semnunon pote lego theon o megille te kai kleinia skhedon ouranon on kai dikaiotaton os sumpantes alloi daimones ama kai theoi timan te kai eukhesthai diapherontos auto to de kai ton allon aition agathon panton emin auton gegonenai pantes an omologoimen dounai de ama kai arithmon emeis ge ontos auton phamen eti de kai dosein ean tis thele sunakolouthein ean gar ie tis epi theorian orthen ten toude eite kosmon eite olumpon eite ouranon en edone to legein legeto men akoloutheito de ope poikillon auton kai ta en auto strephon astra pasas diexodous oras te kai trophen pasin parekhetai kai ten allen de oun phronesin os phaimen an sun arithmo panti kai tall agatha touto de megiston ean tis ten arithmon autou dosin dexamenos epexelthe pasan ten periodon eti de smikron epanelthontes pos tois logois anamnesthomen oti kai mal orthos enoesamen os eiper arithmon ek tes anthropines phuseos exeloimen ouk an pote ti phronimoi genoimetha ou gar an eti pote psukhe toutou tou zoou pasan areten laboi skhedon otou logos apeie zoon de oti me gignoskoi duo kai tria mede peritton mede artion agnooi de to parapan arithmon ouk an pote didonai logon ekhoi peri on aistheseis kai mnemas ekhoi monon eie kektemenon ten de allen areten andreian kai sophrosunen ouden apokoluei steromenos de alethous logou sophos ouk an pote genoito oto de sophia me proseie pases aretes to megiston meros ouk an eti teleos agathos genomenos eudaimon pote genoito outos arithmon men anagke pasa upotithesthai dioti de touto anagke logos eti pleion panton gignoit an ton eiremenon alla kai o nun orthos rethesetai oti kai ta ton allon tekhnon legomena a nunde dielthomen eontes einai pasas tas tekhnas oude touton en ouden menei panta d apoleipetai to parapan otan arithmetiken tis anele doxeie d an isos tis brakheon eneka arithmou deisthai to ton anthropon genos eis tas tekhnas apoblepsas kaitoi mega men kai touto ei de tis idoi to theion tes geneseos kai to thneton en o kai to theosebes gnoristhesetai kai o arithmos ontos ouk an eti pas an tis gnoie sumpanta arithmon oses emin dunameos aitios an eie suggignomenos epei kai ta kata mousiken pasan diarithmoumenon kineseos te kai phthoggon delon oti dei kai to megiston agathon os panton aition oti de kakon oudenos eu touto gnosteon o kai takha genoit an all e skhedon alogistos te kai ataktos askhemon te kai arruthmos anarmostos te phora kai panth oposa kakou kekoinoneken tinos epileleiptai pantos arithmou kai dei touth outo dianoeisthai ton mellonta eudaimona teleutesein kai to ge de dikaion te kai agathon kai kalon kai panta ta toiauta oudeis pote me gignoskon alethous doxes epilabomenos diarithmesetai pros to eauton te kai eteron peisai to parapan iomen de skepsomenoi pros tout auto pos emathomen arithmein phere to gar en de kai duo gegone pothen emin ost ennoesai phusin tauten ekhousin ek tou pantos pros to dunatous ennoein einai pollois de allois au ton zoon oud eis auto touth e phusis paragegonen oste mathein dunatois einai para tou patros arithmein para d emin tout auto proton enokisen o theos oste ikanois einai deiknumenon sunnoein epeit edeixen kai deiknusin on ti kallion en enos an tis theasaito plen to tes emeras genos eita eis to tes nuktos elthoi meros ekhon opsin othen eteron pan auto phainoit an kai elitton de tauta auta otan me pauetai pollas men nuktas pollas de emeras as ouranos oudepote pauetai didaskon anthropous en te kai duo prin an kai o dusmathestatos ikanos mathe arithmein os gar kai tria kai tettara kai polla ekastos emon epinoeseien an oron tauta kai ek touton en epoiesen ten selenen o theos apergasamenos e tote men meizon phainomene tote d elatton diexelthen allen aei phainousa emeran mekhri pentekaideka emeron kai nukton aute d estin periodos ei bouletai tis ton kuklon ena olon eis en tithenai oste os epos eipein kai to dusmathestaton an mathein zoon ois paredoken phusin o theos tou dunatois einai manthanein kai mekhri men touton te kai en toutois sumpan to dunaton ton zoon mala arithmetikon gegone to kath en auto skopoun to de pros allela panta arithmon aei logizesthai doko men meizonos eneka kai toutou de selenen kathaper eipomen auxanomenen kai phthinousan empoiesas menas pros ton eniauton sunestesato kai panta arithmon pros arithmon erxato sunoran eudaimoni tukhe dia de tauth emin karpoi te kai egkumon e ge gegonen ost einai trophen pasi tois zoois anemon te kai ueton gignomenon ouk exaision oude ametron all ei ti para tauta gignetai pros to phlauron ou ten theian alla ten anthropinen aitiasthai khre phusin ouk en dike dianemousan ton auton bion emin d oun zetousin peri nomon skhedon edoxen ta men alla radia t einai gnonai ta beltista anthropois kai pas an ikanos gignesthai kai suneinai ta legomena kai poiein ei gnoie ti pot estin o sumpherein eikos kai ti to me sumpheron edoxe de kai nun eti dokei ta men alla epitedeumata panta ou sphodra khalepa einai to de tina tropon khre gignesthai khrestous anthropous pagkhalepon kai ta men alla au panta ktasthai khresta to legomenon te kai dunaton kai ou khalepon ousian te osen dei kai me dei kai soma oion te dei kai me kai psukhen oti men agathen dei sugkhorei pas panti to d ontina tropon agathen oti men au dikaian kai sophrona kai andreian kai tauta oti de sophen phesi men pas dein entina de sophian os arti dieleluthamen oudeis oudeni to parapan eti sunomologei ton pollon nun oun de para pasas tas prosthen sophias ou phaulen tina aneuriskomen eis auta ge tauta to dokein sophon einai ton ge memathekota aper kai dieleluthamen ei d estin sophos o taut epistemon kai agathos toutou de peri logon dei labein o xene os eikotos eipes oti peri megalon megala epikheireis phrazein ou gar smikra o kleinia to de khalepoteron oti pantapasi kai pantos alethe sphodra ge o xene all omos me apokames legon o phes nai mede spho toinun akouonte taut estai kai uper amphoin ego soi phrazo kalos ex arkhes de reteon anagke proton os phainetai malista men an ei dunametha eni labein onomati tis estin en oiometha sophian einai touto d ei sphodra adunatoumen to deuteron tines eisin pote kai oposai tines as tis labon sophos an eie kata ton emeteron muthon legois an to de meta touto anemeseton to nomothete to kallion ton proteron eiremenon peri theon kai ameinon apeikazonti legein oion paidia kale khromeno kai timonti theous umnois te kai eudaimonia geraironti diagein ton autou bion e kalos o xene legeis ei gar soi touto telos eie ton nomon theous prospaisanti katharoteron de diagagonti ton bion tes ama teleutes aristes te kai kallistes tukhein pos oun o kleinia legomen e dokei tous theous umnountes sphodra timomen eukhomenoi ta kallista kai arista peri auton epienai legein emin outos e pos legeis thaumastos men oun outos all o daimonie pisteusas tois theois eukhou te kai lege ton epionta soi theon ameinon aei kalein o de tropos ode anagke gar to ge tosouton phrazein pan diagramma arithmou te sustema kai armonias sustasin apasan tes te ton astron periphoras ten omologian ousan mian apanton anaphanenai dei to kata tropon manthanonti phanesetai de an o legomen orthos tis eis en blepon manthane desmos gar pephukos panton touton eis anaphanesetai dianooumenois ei d allos pos tauta metakheirieitai tis tukhen dei kalein osper kai legomen ou gar aneu ge touton mepote tis en polesin eudaimon genetai phusis all outos o tropos aute e trophe tauta ta mathemata eite khalepa eite radia taute poreuteon amelesai de ou themiton estin theon kataphanous genomenes tes panton auton kata tropon legomenes phemes eutukhous ton de sumpanta tauta outos eilephota touton lego ton alethestata sophotaton on kai diiskhurizomai paizon kai spoudazon ama ote thanato tis ton toiouton ten autou moiran anaplesei skhedon eanper et apothanon e mete methexein eti pollon tote kathaper nun aistheseon mias te moiras meteilephota monon kai ek pollon ena gegonota eudaimona te esesthai kai sophotaton ama kai makarion eite tis en epeirois eit en nesois makarios on ze kakeinon methexein tes toiautes aei tukhes keite demosia tis epitedeusas tauta eite idia diabio ta auta kai osautos auton praxein para theon o de kat arkhas te elegomen kai nun autos paresti logos alethes ontos os ou dunaton anthropois teleos makariois te kai eudaimosi genesthai plen oligon estin tauta orthos eiremena oposoi gar theioi kai sophrones ama tes alles te metekhontes aretes phusei pros de toutois osa mathematos ekhetai makariou panta eilephotes a d estin eirekamen toutoisin monois ta tou daimoniou sumpanta ikanos eilekhe te kai ekhei tois men oun tauta outo diaponesasin idia legomen kai demosia kata nomon tithemen eis presbutou telos aphikomenois tas megistas arkhas paradidosthai dein tous d allous toutois sunepomenous euphemein pantas theous ama kai pasas kai ton nukterinon sullogon epi tauten ten sophian ikanos gnontas te kai dokimasantas emas orthotata pantas parakalein
-1 Cleitophon kleitophonta ton aristonumou tis emin diegeito enagkhos oti lusia dialegomenos tas men meta sokratous diatribas psegoi ten thrasumakhou de sunousian uperepainoi ostis o sokrates ouk orthos apemnemoneue soi tous emoi peri sou genomenous logous pros lusian ta men gar egoge ouk epenoun se ta de kai epenoun epei de delos ei memphomenos men moi prospoioumenos de meden phrontizein edist an soi diexelthoimi autous autos epeide kai mono tugkhanomen onte ina etton me ege pros se phaulos ekhein nun gar isos ouk orthos akekoas oste phaine pros eme ekhein trakhuteros tou deontos ei de moi didos parresian edista an dexaimen kai ethelo legein all aiskhron men sou ge ophelein me prothumoumenou me upomenein delon gar os gnous ope kheiron eimi kai beltion ta men askeso kai dioxomai ta de pheuxomai kata kratos akouois an ego gar o sokrates soi suggignomenos pollakis exeplettomen akouon kai moi edokeis para tous allous anthropous kallista legein opote epitimon tois anthropois osper epi mekhanes tragikes theos umneis legon poi pheresthe onthropoi kai agnoeite ouden ton deonton prattontes oitines khrematon men peri ten pasan spouden ekhete opos umin estai ton d ueon ois tauta paradosete opos epistesontai khresthai dikaios toutois oute didaskalous autois euriskete tes dikaiosunes eiper matheton ei de meleteton te kai asketon oitines exaskesousin kai ekmeletesousin ikanos oude g eti proteron umas autous outos etherapeusate all orontes grammata kai mousiken kai gumnastiken umas te autous kai tous paidas umon ikanos memathekotas a de paideian aretes einai telean egeisthe kapeita ouden etton kakous gignomenous peri ta khremata pos ou kataphroneite tes nun paideuseos oude zeteite oitines umas pausousi tautes tes amousias kaitoi dia ge tauten ten plemmeleian kai rathumian all ou dia ten en to podi pros ten luran ametrian kai adelphos adelpho kai poleis polesin ametros kai anarmostos prospheromenai stasiazousi kai polemountes ta eskhata drosin kai paskhousin umeis de phate ou di apaideusian oude di agnoian all ekontas tous adikous adikous einai palin d au tolmate legein os aiskhron kai theomises e adikia pos oun de tis to ge toiouton kakon ekon airoit an etton os an e phate ton edonon oukoun kai touto akousion eiper to nikan ekousion oste ek pantos tropou to ge adikein akousion o logos airei kai dein epimeleian tes nun pleio poieisthai pant andra idia th ama kai demosia sumpasas tas poleis taut oun o sokrates ego otan akouo sou thama legontos kai mala agamai kai thaumastos os epaino kai opotan au phes to ephexes touto tous askountas men ta somata tes de psukhes emelekotas eteron ti prattein toiouton tou men arxontos amelein peri de to arxomenon espoudakenai kai otan leges os oto tis me epistatai khresthai kreitton ean ten toutou khresin ei de tis me epistatai ophthalmois khresthai mede osin mede sumpanti to somati touto mete akouein meth oran met allen khreian medemian khresthai to somati kreitton e opeoun khresthai kai de kai peri tekhnen osautos ostis gar de me epistatai te eautou lura khresthai delon os oude te tou geitonos oude ostis me te ton allon oude te eautou oud allo ton organon oude ktematon oudeni kai teleuta de kalos o logos outos soi os ostis psukhe me epistatai khresthai touto to agein esukhian te psukhe kai me zen kreitton e zen prattonti kath auton ei de tis anagke zen eie doulo ameinon e eleuthero diagein to toiouto ton bion estin ara kathaper ploiou paradonti ta pedalia tes dianoias allo to mathonti ten ton anthropon kubernetiken en de su politiken o sokrates eponomazeis pollakis ten auten de tauten dikastiken te kai dikaiosunen os estin legon toutois de tois logois kai eterois toioutois pampollois kai pagkalos legomenois os didakton arete kai panton eautou dei malista epimeleisthai skhedon out anteipon popote out oimai mepote usteron anteipo protreptikotatous te egoumai kai ophelimotatous kai atekhnos osper katheudontas epegeirein emas proseikhon de ton noun to meta tauta os akousomenos epaneroton outi se to proton o sokrates alla ton elikioton te kai sunepithumeton e etairon son e opos dei pros se peri auton to toiouton onomazein touton gar tous ti malista einai doxazomenous upo sou protous epaneroton punthanomenos tis o meta taut eie logos kai kata se tropon tina upoteinon autois o beltistoi ephen umeis pos pote nun apodekhometha ten sokratous protropen emon ep areten os ontos monou toutou epexelthein de ouk eni to pragmati kai labein auto teleos all emin para panta de ton bion ergon tout estai tous mepo protetrammenous protrepein kai ekeinous au eterous e dei ton sokrate kai allelous emas to meta tout epanerotan omologesantas tout auto anthropo prakteon einai ti tounteuthen pos arkhesthai dein phamen dikaiosunes peri matheseos osper an ei tis emas proutrepen tou somatos epimeleian poieisthai meden pronoountas oron kathaper paidas os estin tis gumnastike kai iatrike kapeita oneidizen legon os aiskhron puron men kai krithon kai ampelon epimeleian pasan poieisthai kai osa tou somatos eneka diaponoumetha te kai ktometha toutou d autou medemian tekhnen mede mekhanen opos os beltiston estai to soma exeuriskein kai tauta ousan ei d epanerometha ton tauth emas protreponta legeis de einai tinas tautas tas tekhnas eipen an isos oti gumnastike kai iatrike kai nun de tina phamen einai ten epi te tes psukhes arete tekhnen legestho o de dokon auton erromenestatos einai pros tauta apokrinomenos eipen moi tauten ten tekhnen einai enper akoueis su legontos ephe sokratous ouk allen e dikaiosunen eipontos d emou me moi to onoma monon eipes alla ode iatrike pou tis legetai tekhne tautes d estin ditta ta apoteloumena to men iatrous aei pros tois ousin eterous exergazesthai to de ugieian estin de touton thateron ouketi tekhne tes tekhnes de tes didaskouses te kai didaskomenes ergon o de legomen ugieian kai tektonikes de kata tauta oikia te kai tektonike to men ergon to de didagma tes de dikaiosunes osautos to men dikaious esto poiein kathaper ekei tous tekhnitas ekastous to d eteron o dunatai poiein emin ergon o dikaios ti touto phamen eipe outos men os oimai to sumpheron apekrinato allos de to deon eteros de to ophelimon o de to lusiteloun epaneein de ego legon oti kakei ta ge onomata taut estin en ekaste ton tekhnon orthos prattein lusitelounta ophelima kai talla ta toiauta alla pros oti tauta panta teinei erei to idion ekaste e tekhne oion e tektonike to eu to kalos to deontos oste ta xulina phesei skeue gignesthai a de ouk estin tekhne legestho de kai to tes dikaiosunes osautos teleuton apekrinato tis o sokrates moi ton son etairon os de kompsotata edoxen eipein oti tout eie to tes dikaiosunes idion ergon o ton allon oudemias philian en tais polesin poiein outos d au erotomenos ten philian agathon t ephe einai kai oudepote kakon tas de ton paidon philias kai tas ton therion as emeis touto tounoma eponomazomen ouk apedekheto einai philias epanerotomenos sunebaine gar auto ta pleio tas toiautas blaberas e agathas einai pheugon de to toiouton oude philias ephe tas toiautas einai pseudos de onomazein autas tous outos onomazontas ten de ontos kai alethos philian einai saphestata omonoian ten de omonoian erotomenos ei omodoxian einai legoi e epistemen ten men omodoxian etimazen enagkazonto gar pollai kai blaberai gignesthai omodoxiai anthropon ten de philian agathon omologekei pantos einai kai dikaiosunes ergon oste tauton ephesen einai omonoian kai epistemen ousan all ou doxan ote de entautha emen tou logou aporountes oi parontes ikanoi esan epiplettein te auto kai legein oti peridedrameken eis tauton o logos tois protois kai elegon oti kai e iatrike omonoia tis esti kai apasai ai tekhnai kai peri otou eisin ekhousi legein ten de upo sou legomenen dikaiosunen e omonoian opoi teinousa estin diapepheugen kai adelon autes oti pot estin to ergon tauta o sokrates ego teleuton kai se auton eroton kai eipes moi dikaiosunes einai tous men ekhthrous blaptein tous de philous eu poiein usteron de ephane blaptein ge oudepote o dikaios oudena panta gar ep ophelia pantas dran tauta de oukh apax oude dis alla polun de upomeinas khronon kai liparon apeireka nomisas se to men protrepein eis aretes epimeleian kallist anthropon dran duoin de thateron e tosouton monon dunasthai makroteron de ouden o genoit an kai peri allen entinaoun tekhnen oion me onta kuberneten katameletesai ton epainon peri autes os pollou tois anthropois axia kai peri ton allon tekhnon osautos tauton de kai soi tis epenegkoi takh an peri dikaiosunes os ou mallon onti dikaiosunes epistemoni dioti kalos auten egkomiazeis ou men to ge emon outos ekhei duoin de thateron e ouk eidenai se e ouk ethelein autes emoi koinonein dia tauta de kai pros thrasumakhon oimai poreusomai kai allose opoi dunamai aporon epei ei g etheleis su touton men ede pausasthai pros eme ton logon ton protreptikon oion de ei peri gumnastikes protetrammenos e tou somatos dein me amelein to ephexes an to protreptiko logo eleges oion to soma mou phusei on oias therapeias deitai kai nun de tauton gignestho thes ton kleitophonta omologounta os estin katagelaston ton men allon epimeleian poieisthai psukhes de es eneka talla diaponoumetha tautes emelekenai kai talla panta oiou me nun outos eirekenai ta toutois exes a kai nunde dielthon kai sou deomenos lego medamos allos poiein ina me kathaper nun ta men epaino se pros lusian kai pros tous allous ta de ti kai psego me men gar protetrammeno se anthropo o sokrates axion einai tou pantos pheso protetrammeno de skhedon kai empodion tou pros telos aretes elthonta eudaimona genesthai
